Reporting This report adheres core standard Global Reporting Initiative(GRI) Standards. creating this report, also referred ISO 26000, principles UN Global Compact, Guideline international integrated reporting framework International Integrated Reporting Council(IIRC). financial standards definitions presented this report align Korean-International Financial Reporting Standards(K-IFRS). addition, this report contains recommendations from Task-force Climate-related Financial Disclosures(TCFD). industry standards Sustainability Accounting Standards Board(SASB) were also taken into consideration order reflect material issues within electric industry. Reporting This report covers our activities performance from January , 2021 December 31, 2021. have provided data first half 2021 qualitative activities related several major Period issues. identify changes trend qualitative performance, are disclosing data last three years (2019-2021). accordance our disclosure approach, report presents both financial non-finnacial information fiscal year. Furthermore, any information that does not meet aforementioned standards has been labeled such form separate comments. Scope This report shares local international ESG performance six other generation companies(Korea Hydro & Nuclear Co., Ltd; Korea South-East Co., Report Ltd; Korea Midland Co., Ltd; Korea Western Co., Ltd; Korea Southern Co., Ltd; Korea East-West Co., Ltd.) (hereafter, KHNP, KOEN, KOMIPO, KOWEPO, KOSPO, EWP) financial information included herein is reported accordance K-IFR's independent financial statements, contents consolidated standards are denoted separate comments. Independent commissioned professional verification agency, Korea Sustainability Reporting Institute (KOSRI), third-party verification ensure report's internal external reliability. Code Conduct Suppliers is based 10 principles United Nations Global Compact(UNGC), OECD Due Diligence Guideline Fundamental Conventions defines specifies ethical, environmental, social standards. It provides guidance all domestic foreign partners business relationships , along their employees, agents sub-contractor s ask them comply guideline. Details Code Conducts Suppliers Ethical Standards • No bribery including money • No solicitation benefits one's own or others other valuables • Ethical education corruption • No unfair trade including collusion reports Social Standards • Prohibition discrimination • Compliance domestic employment foreign tax labor laws • Guaranteeing freedom assembly • Prohibition o f child labor association right collective bargaining • Provision safety equipment Environmental • No bribery including money safe work environments other valuables Standards • Environmentally-conscious • No unfair trade including collusion activities Supply Chain ESG Risk is reflecting non-financial risk evaluation indicators existing supply chain evaluation process diagnose improve non- financial(ESG) risks within supply chain. Non-financial risk evaluation indicators include economic indicators such credit rating, equipment quality rating, quality (ISO 19001) certification, environmental indicators such eco-friendly product certification, production environment violation environmental laws, social indicators such sanctions anti- corruption subcontracting law violation, safety accidents, safety equipment securing. Supply chain evaluation is conducted written evaluation -site inspection. written evaluation is evaluation based responses evidence(data, etc.) submitted suppliers each evaluation index at time contract bidding, is used basic data identify potential risks suppliers. addition, low performers quality evaluation, test evaluate equipment performance quality inspection are conducted prevent quality risk.
